Built with Alectryon, running Coq+SerAPI v8.20.0+0.20.0. Bubbles () indicate interactive fragments: hover for details, tap to reveal contents. Use Ctrl+↑ Ctrl+↓ to navigate, Ctrl+🖱️ to focus. On Mac, use ⌘ instead of Ctrl.
(**** ZF Structures

    Dimitris Tsementzis (@dimtsem), Feb. 2018

Main contents of this file:

         - A definition of "ZF structures" as well-founded rooted trees with no automorphisms plus
           some extra properties [ZFS]
         - A proof that the type [ZFS] of ZF structures is an h-set [isaset_ZFS]
         - A definition of the elementhood relation for ZF structures [ZFS_elementof]

Table of Contents:
      (1) Auxilliary Lemmas
      (2) Basic Definitions
      (3) Definition of ZFS
      (4) The Elementhood Relation

A textbook reference for some of the material in this file can be found in:
         - Mac Lane and Moerdijk, "Sheaves in Geometry and Logic", VI.10

****)

X: UU
P: X → hProp
T: ∑ x : X, P x
C: iscontr (T = T)
iscontr (pr1 T = pr1 T)

P: X → hProp
T: ∑ x : X, P x
C: iscontr (T = T)
iscontr (pr1 T = pr1 T)

  exact (@isofhlevelweqf 0 (T = T) (pr1 T = pr1 T) (@total2_paths_hProp_equiv _ _ T T) C).
Qed.

S: UU
iso: S → S → UU
u: ∏ X Y : S, X = Y ≃ iso X Y
Q: S → hProp
A, B: ∑ X : S, Q X
A = B ≃ iso (pr1 A) (pr1 B)


S: UU
iso: S → S → UU
u: ∏ X Y : S, X = Y ≃ iso X Y

A = B ≃ iso (pr1 A) (pr1 B)

  
S: UU
iso: S → S → UU
u: ∏ X Y : S, X = Y ≃ iso X Y

A, B: ∑ X : S, Q X
A = B ≃ pr1 A = pr1 B
S: UU
iso: S → S → UU
u: ∏ X Y : S, X = Y ≃ iso X Y
Q: S → hProp
A, B: ∑ X : S, Q X
pr1 A = pr1 B ≃ iso (pr1 A) (pr1 B)

  
S: UU
iso: S → S → UU
u: ∏ X Y : S, X = Y ≃ iso X Y
Q: S → hProp
A, B: ∑ X : S, Q X
pr1 A = pr1 B ≃ iso (pr1 A) (pr1 B)

  apply (u (pr1 A) (pr1 B)).
Qed.

(** The definition of transitive reflexive rooted graphs [TRRGraph] **)

Definition PointedGraph := ∑ (V : hSet) (E : hrel V), V.

Definition isaroot {V : hSet} (E : hrel V) (r : V) : UU := (∏ w : V, E r w).

 apply propproperty.
Qed.

Definition isTRR (V : hSet) (E : hrel V) (r : V) : UU :=
  isrefl E × istrans E × isaroot E r.

Definition TRRGraph : UU := ∑ (V : hSet), TRRGraphData V.

Definition TRRG_edgerel (G : TRRGraph) : hrel (pr1 G) := pr12 G.


Setting y constr at next level
to match previous notation with longest common prefix:
"_ ≤ _".


Definition TRRG_root (G : TRRGraph) : pr1 G := pr122 G.

Definition TRRG_transitivity (G : TRRGraph) : istrans (TRRG_edgerel G) := pr12 (pr222 G).

Definition selfedge (G : TRRGraph) (x : pr1 G) : pr1 (pr2 G) x x :=
  (pr1 (pr2 (pr2 (pr2 G))) x).

(** Definition of [TRRGraph] homomorphisms [isTRRGhomo], isomorphisms [TRRGraphiso], and a proof
    that isomorphisms are equivalent to identities [TRRGraph_univalence] **)

Definition isTRRGhomo {G H : TRRGraph} (f : pr1 G → pr1 H) : UU :=
  (∏ (x y : pr1 G), (x ≤ y) <-> (f x ≤ f y)) × (f (TRRG_root G) = TRRG_root H).


G, H: TRRGraph
f: pr1 G → pr1 H
isaprop (isTRRGhomo f)

Qed.

Definition TRRGraphiso (G H : TRRGraph) : UU := ∑ (f : pr1 G ≃ pr1 H), isTRRGhomo f.

Definition TRRGraph_univalence_weq1 (G H : TRRGraph) : G = H ≃ G ╝ H :=
  total2_paths_equiv _ G H.


G, H: TRRGraph
G ╝ H ≃ G ≅ H


G, H: TRRGraph
G ╝ H ≃ G ≅ H

  
G, H: TRRGraph
pr1 G = pr1 H ≃ (pr1 G ≃ pr1 H)

 transportf (λ x1 : hSet, TRRGraphData x1) x0 (pr2 G) =
 pr2 H) x
≃ (λ x0 : pr1 G ≃ pr1 H, isTRRGhomo x0) (?w x)

pr1 G = pr1 H ≃ (pr1 G ≃ pr1 H)

 pr2 H) x

    (hSet_univalence (pr1 G) (pr1 H) x)

(** Definition of trees as a subtype [Tree] of [TRRGraph] and proof of univalence for trees
    [Tree_univalence] **)

Definition DownwardClosure {G : TRRGraph} (x : pr1 G) : UU :=
  ∑ y : pr1 G, y ≤ x.

Definition antisymmetric {G :TRRGraph} (y z : pr1 G) : UU :=
  (y ≤ z) × (z ≤ y) → (z = y).

Definition total {G : TRRGraph} (y z : pr1 G) : hProp :=
  (y ≤ z) ∨ (z ≤ y).

Definition isatree (G : TRRGraph) : UU :=
  ∏ (x : pr1 G) (y z : DownwardClosure x), antisymmetric (pr1 y) (pr1 z) × total (pr1 y) (pr1 z).


G: TRRGraph
isaprop (isatree G)


G: TRRGraph
isaprop (isatree G)

  
G: TRRGraph
∏ t : pr1 G,
isofhlevel 1
  (∏ y z : DownwardClosure t,
   antisymmetric (pr1 y) (pr1 z)
   × total (pr1 y) (pr1 z))

  
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
∏ t0 : DownwardClosure t,
isofhlevel 1
  (∏ z : DownwardClosure t,
   antisymmetric (pr1 t0) (pr1 z)
   × total (pr1 t0) (pr1 z))

  
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x: DownwardClosure t
∏ t : DownwardClosure t,
isofhlevel 1
  (antisymmetric (pr1 x) (pr1 t)
   × total (pr1 x) (pr1 t))

  
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
isaprop (antisymmetric (pr1 x) (pr1 y))
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
isaprop (total (pr1 x) (pr1 y))

  
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
isaprop (antisymmetric (pr1 x) (pr1 y))
 
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
pr1 x ≤ pr1 y × pr1 y ≤ pr1 x
→ isofhlevel 1 (pr1 y = pr1 x)

    
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
P: pr1 x ≤ pr1 y × pr1 y ≤ pr1 x
isofhlevel 1 (pr1 y = pr1 x)

    apply setproperty.
  
G: TRRGraph
t: pr1 G
x, y: DownwardClosure t
isaprop (total (pr1 x) (pr1 y))
 apply propproperty.
Qed.

Definition Tree : UU :=  ∑ G : TRRGraph, isatree G.

Definition Tree_iso (T1 T2 : Tree) : UU := pr1 T1 ≅ pr1 T2.


T1, T2: Tree
T1 = T2 ≃ Tree_iso T1 T2


T1, T2: Tree
T1 = T2 ≃ Tree_iso T1 T2

  
T1, T2: Tree
P:= λ G H : TRRGraph, TRRGraph_univalence G H: ∏ G H : TRRGraph, G = H ≃ G ≅ H
T1 = T2 ≃ Tree_iso T1 T2

  
T1, T2: Tree
P:= λ G H : TRRGraph, TRRGraph_univalence G H: ∏ G H : TRRGraph, G = H ≃ G ≅ H
Q:= λ G : TRRGraph, isatree G,, isaprop_isatree G: TRRGraph → ∑ y, isaprop y
T1 = T2 ≃ Tree_iso T1 T2

  apply (substructure_univalence _ _ P Q T1 T2).
Qed.

(** Definition of branches ("upward closures") for [Tree]s as a tree [Up x] for a point x of T **)

Definition Upw_underlying (T : Tree) (x : pr11 T) := ∑ (y : pr11 T), x ≤ y.

Qed.

Definition Upw (T : Tree) (x : pr11 T) : hSet :=
  (∑ (y : pr11 T), pr121 T x y) ,, (isaset_Upw_underlying T x).

Definition Upw_E (T : Tree) (x : pr11 T) (y z : Upw T x) : hProp :=
  pr121 T (pr1 y) (pr1 z).

Definition Upw_to_PointedGraph (T : Tree) (x : pr11 T) : PointedGraph :=
  Upw T x ,, Upw_E T x ,, (x ,, selfedge (pr1 T) x).

(pr12 (Upw_to_PointedGraph T x)) y y

Definition Up {T : Tree} (x : pr11 T) : Tree := (Upw_to_TRRGraph T x ,, isatree_Upw T x).

(** Definition of rigid [isrigid] and superrigid [issuperrigid] trees **)

Definition isrigid (T : Tree) : UU
  := iscontr (T = T).


T: Tree
isaprop (isrigid T)


T: Tree
isaprop (isrigid T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (iscontr (T = T))

  apply isapropiscontr.
Qed.

Definition issuperrigid (T : Tree) : UU :=
  isrigid T × (∏ (x : pr11 T), isrigid (Up x)).


T: Tree
isaprop (issuperrigid T)


T: Tree
isaprop (issuperrigid T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (isrigid T × (∏ x : pr11 T, isrigid (Up x)))

  
T: Tree
isaprop (isrigid T)
T: Tree
isaprop (∏ x : pr11 T, isrigid (Up x))

  
T: Tree
isaprop (∏ x : pr11 T, isrigid (Up x))

  
T: Tree
∏ t : pr11 T, isofhlevel 1 (isrigid (Up t))

  
T: Tree
t: pr11 T
isofhlevel 1 (isrigid (Up t))

  apply isaprop_isrigid.
Qed.

(** Definition of bi-well-founded trees (well-founded both "up" and "down") [Tree_isWellFounded] **)

Definition isWellFoundedUp (T : Tree) : hProp :=
  hasSmallest (pr121 T).

Definition hasLargest {X : UU} (R : hrel X) : hProp :=
  ∀ S : hsubtype X, (∃ x, S x) ⇒ ∃ x:X, S x ∧ ∀ y:X, S y ⇒ R y x.

Definition isWellFoundedDown (T : Tree) := hasLargest (pr121 T).

Definition Tree_isWellFounded (T : Tree) := (isWellFoundedUp T) × (isWellFoundedDown T).


T: Tree
isaprop (Tree_isWellFounded T)


T: Tree
isaprop (Tree_isWellFounded T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (isWellFoundedUp T)
T: Tree
isaprop (isWellFoundedDown T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (isWellFoundedDown T)

  apply propproperty.
Qed.

(** The definition of pre-ZF structures [preZFS]. **)

(**

   [preZFS] is classically equivalent to the [ZFS] we define below but, as far as we can tell,
   constructively inequivalent.

**)

Definition ispreZFS (T : Tree) : UU := (Tree_isWellFounded T) × (issuperrigid T).


T: Tree
isaprop (ispreZFS T)


T: Tree
isaprop (ispreZFS T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (Tree_isWellFounded T)
T: Tree
isaprop (issuperrigid T)

  
T: Tree
isaprop (issuperrigid T)

  apply (isaprop_issuperrigid T).
Qed.

Definition preZFS : UU := ∑ (T : Tree), ispreZFS T.

Definition Ve (X : preZFS) : hSet := pr111 X.
Coercion Ve : preZFS >-> hSet.

Definition Ed (X : preZFS) : (Ve X) → (Ve X) → hProp := pr1 (pr2 (pr1 (pr1 X))).

Definition root (X : preZFS) : Ve X := pr1 (pr2 (pr2 (pr1 (pr1 X)))).


X: preZFS
iscontr (X = X)


X: preZFS
iscontr (X = X)

  
X: preZFS
iscontr (pr1 X = pr1 X)

  exact (pr122 X).
Qed.


isaset preZFS


isaset preZFS

  
isaset preZFS

  
∏ x x' : preZFS, isaprop (x = x')

  
∏ x x' : preZFS, isofhlevel 1 (x = x')

  
∏ (x x' : preZFS) (x0 x'0 : x = x'),
iscontr (x0 = x'0)

  
x, y: preZFS
p: x = y
∏ x' : x = y, iscontr (p = x')

  
x: preZFS
∏ x' : x = x, iscontr (idpath x = x')

  
x: preZFS
q: x = x
iscontr (idpath x = q)

  apply (hlevelntosn 0 (x = x) (preZFS_isrigid x) (idpath x) q).
Qed.

Definition preZFS_iso (X Y : preZFS) : UU := Tree_iso (pr1 X) (pr1 Y).


X, Y: preZFS
X = Y ≃ preZFS_iso X Y


X, Y: preZFS
X = Y ≃ preZFS_iso X Y

  
X, Y: preZFS
P:= λ x y : Tree, Tree_univalence x y: ∏ x y : Tree, x = y ≃ Tree_iso x y
X = Y ≃ preZFS_iso X Y

  
X, Y: preZFS
P:= λ x y : Tree, Tree_univalence x y: ∏ x y : Tree, x = y ≃ Tree_iso x y
Q:= λ x : Tree, ispreZFS x,, isaprop_ispreZFS x: Tree → ∑ y, isaprop y
X = Y ≃ preZFS_iso X Y

  exact (substructure_univalence _ _ P Q X Y).
Qed.

(*** End of Basic Definitions ***)

(*** Definition of ZFS ***)

(** Contents **)

(**
-Upward Closure ("Branch") of a node x in a pre-ZF structure T
-Proof that it is a pre-ZF structure [Branch]
**)

Definition preZFS_Branch (T : preZFS) (x : T) : Tree := Up x.

Definition preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype (T : preZFS) (x : T)
           (S : hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))) : hsubtype (pr111 T) :=
  λ t, ∃ e, S (t ,, e).

(**
REMARK : The definition [preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype] probably does not need to be
truncated. One can define it without truncation and prove the lemmas that it is a proposition.
**)

Definition hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype (T : preZFS) (x : T) (S : hsubtype (pr111 T)) :
  hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x)) := λ z, S (pr1 z) ∧ Ed T x (pr1 z).


T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S) = S


T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S) = S

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H = S

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
homotsec H S

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
∏ x : pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x), H x = S x

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
y: pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x)
H y = S y

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
y: pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x)
H y = S y

  
T: preZFS
x: T
S: hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))
H:= hsubtype_to_preZFS_Branch_hsubtype T x
  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))

H y = S y

  
T: preZFS
x: T

  (preZFS_Branch_hsubtype_tohsubtype T x S): hsubtype (pr11 (preZFS_Branch T x))

H y = S y

Definition Branch (T : preZFS) (x : T) : preZFS :=
  preZFS_Branch T x ,, preZFS_Branch_isWellFounded T x ,, preZFS_Branch_issuperrigid T x.

(** The definition of [ZFS] as a subtype of [preZFS] consisting of those pre-ZF structures each of
    whose branches have uniqe representatives [hasuniquerepbranch] **)

Definition hasuniquerepbranch (T : preZFS) : UU :=
  ∏ (x y : T), (Branch T x) = (Branch T y) → x = y.


T: preZFS
isaprop (hasuniquerepbranch T)


T: preZFS
isaprop (hasuniquerepbranch T)

  
T: preZFS
t, t0: T
t1: Branch T t = Branch T t0
isofhlevel 1 (t = t0)

  apply setproperty.
Qed.

Definition ZFS : UU := ∑ (X : preZFS), hasuniquerepbranch X.

Definition pr1ZFS (X : ZFS) : preZFS := pr1 X.
Coercion pr1ZFS : ZFS >-> preZFS.

Definition ZFS_iso (x y : ZFS) := preZFS_iso x y.


x, y: ZFS
x = y ≃ ZFS_iso x y


x, y: ZFS
x = y ≃ ZFS_iso x y

  
x, y: ZFS
P:= λ x y : preZFS, preZFS_univalence x y: ∏ x y : preZFS, x = y ≃ preZFS_iso x y
x = y ≃ ZFS_iso x y

  
x, y: ZFS
P:= λ x y : preZFS, preZFS_univalence x y: ∏ x y : preZFS, x = y ≃ preZFS_iso x y
Q:= λ x : preZFS,
hasuniquerepbranch x,, isaprop_hasuniquerepbranch x: preZFS → ∑ y, isaprop y
x = y ≃ ZFS_iso x y

  apply (substructure_univalence _ _ P Q x y).
Qed.

Definition ZFS_Branch (X : ZFS) (x : X) : ZFS := (Branch X x ,, ZFS_Branch_is_ZFS X x).

Local Notation "T ↑ x" := (ZFS_Branch T x)(at level 40).

Local Notation "x ⊏ y" := ((pr121 (pr111 _)) x y)(at level 50).

Definition Root (X : ZFS) := pr122 (pr111 X).

Definition isapoint {X : ZFS} (x : X) := ¬ (x = Root X).

Qed.

Definition ZFS_elementof (X Y : ZFS) := ∑ (a : Y), (isapoint a) × (X = Y ↑ a).
